However, your high Narcissism indicates a strong sense of self-importance and a need for admiration, which can sometimes lead to grandiose behavior and a tendency to prioritize your own needs above others. Meanwhile, your low Psychopathy suggests that you are not devoid of empathy, and you may be more likely to form meaningful connections with others, even if you do struggle with impulsivity and a lack of emotional regulation. This combination can result in a complex and sometimes contradictory personality, where you may be both charismatic and self-centered, yet also vulnerable and emotionally intense.

Meanwhile, your low Psychopathy suggests that you are not devoid of empathy, and you may be more likely to form meaningful connections with others, even if you do struggle with impulsivity and a lack of emotional regulation. This combination can result in a complex and sometimes contradictory personality, where you may be both charismatic and self-centered, yet also vulnerable and emotionally intense.
